# Opera AI Practice Management System - Complete Dataset
# Generated: 2025-09-20T04:51:37.375Z
# This dataset contains comprehensive practice data for AI analysis

## SYSTEM CONTEXT
This is a dental/orthodontic practice management system with the following data types:
- APPOINTMENT_BOOKINGS: Patient appointments with dates, times, and details
- PATIENTS: Patient demographic and contact information
- APPOINTMENT_TYPES: Different types of services offered
- LOCATIONS: Practice locations and addresses
- PATIENT_TREATMENTS: Treatment records and procedures

## DATA FORMAT INSTRUCTIONS
Each record follows this format: [ENTITY_TYPE] [ID] [DATE] [JSON_DATA]
The AI should analyze this data to answer questions about:
- Practice performance and statistics
- Patient demographics and patterns
- Appointment scheduling and trends
- Business insights and recommendations
- Operational efficiency and optimization
